Hard or soft, shrill or harmonious, classic or capricious. \r\nA midi file is a collection of sheet music for a whole orchestra with up to 16 voices (= instruments or sounds). The notes for each voice are hold in a track and you can assign an arbitrary sound to each track to give it its specific character. So you can arrange the song in a creative way and create and publish your own interpretations.\r\nMany of the midi files are free (for example: Mutopia Project with tousends of songs), others are copyright protected and have to be purchased.\r\nThe SoundDesigner Music Creator contains a collection of 4 synthesizer engines: GM Bank, Additive Synthesizer, Waveform Modulator and Sampler. It can also import preset sounds from the SoundDesigner and the Dynamic Synth and sound samples. First steps:\r\n1) Load a midi file (or a project).\r\n2) Assign sounds to the different tracks. (Select a track and then select the sounds).\r\n3) Test (play) the track and than test the whole song (play all).\r\n4) If you want, you can add special effects to the tracks (optional).\r\n5) Play or
